< Text>
I spent two months trying to troubleshoot a non-functioning sauna heater, and was laughed off the phone by company after company when I mentioned we live in Bolinas. I was able to narrow down the issue, ordered replacement parts, and luckily John Owens Services was able to book an appointment and take on the job. <userid>118144797646489058097<//userid>< username>
Nancy Zeravich<//username>
<date>1581278215165< /date><rating>5< /rating><text>This is our first encounter with John Owns Services. We were referred to them from the Trane Website as our local dealer to help install a new Trane Air Conditioning Unit to our existing Trane Forced-Air Heater.

Chris, HVAC designer came out the same day and assessed our 1974 home. He determined that we needed to update our vents to provide the best air flow. No other HVAC contractor mentioned this important factor. He also recommended the best size of unit for our needs.

Alex, project manager, came out the next day to perform a thorough assessment of our existing system including specific measurements and drawings to assist the installation team. His thoroughness is impressive.

Juan and Angel performed the installation. They are amazing. They are a true team. They enjoy their work (which is dirty and dangerous) and want to provide the same level of professionalism and craftsmanship as if it were their own home.

They took it upon themselves to remodel our basement area in order to create the best, most serviceable area for our Heating and Air Conditioning systems. This required relocating the existing Heating Unit, installing new/larger electrical service, etc which required 100' runs under the house!

The basement area is just about inaccessible. It is located at the opposite end of our home which is on a very steep hillside. Every trip with materials, etc. had to be hand carried about 100' from our driveway.

In order to carry the huge Trane A/C unit they dug a 50 foot dirt trail along the steep hillside. With each of them on opposite sides of the heavy, awkward unit they, and two helpers, painstakingly maneuvered the unit down dangerous, uneven stairs and along the dirt trail and underneath a wooden deck to the correct position. It was like watching an act from Cirque de Soleil.

According to Alex, this type of installation would normally take at least three days. Juan and Angel, working 10 to 12 hour days, completed it in two.

We needed to install a new return which was over 85 feet long. We also needed a new floor register. Each situation required on the spot innovation and design decisions.

Juan and Angel never complained nor appeared to require hand-holding from management. They adapted.

At the end of the day, a contractor is as good as his sub-contractors. In this case, John Owens is very fortunate to have found such dedicated and skilled craftsman.

We feel good about supporting a local San Rafael contractor! John Owens can provide warranty service, as well as, a wide variety of other contracting services and that makes us feel secure.

Thank you Chris, Alex, Juan and Angel. We remember you every time we use our Trane System!

John and Nancy Zeravich<//text>< pictures>

<user_id>109757733254862782119< /user_id><user_name>Tex Austin<//user_name>< date>
1575186823829</date>
<Rating>5<//Rating>< Text>
I've been remiss in not having posted this review in September, when JOHN OWENS SERVICES came to our rescue.  And, while I want to emphasize what a great company I've found John Owens Services to be, I want to set the back story of how I found them.

My wife and I had a Trane central heating and air conditioning system installed in a portion of our home by a Novato Trane dealer in 2017.  In July, 2019, during that company's annual System Maintenance Inspection, we mentioned to their lead technician that during the cooling cycle, unlike during the past two summers, the system's fan was putting out an incredible rush of air and associated noise from our registers. It was so loud that it was difficult to carry on a normal conversation at our dining table, and it made it necessary for us to use ear plugs to sleep during the hot nights.

I asked the technician if the flow rate could have somehow been switched from a lower level.  He said that wasn't possible, that nothing could be done, and that he thought the unit they'd installed was too large for that part of our house.

In early August, I contacted the Company's owner/office manager to tell her about our problem.  At her request, I emailed her a video, showing the situation, and she said that they'd get back to me on the following Monday. Not hearing back for a week, I called again, and she said her husband was out of the office, but that she'd let him know I'd called.  Again, never hearing back, I called and left messages several more times over the next month.

Finally, after two months of complete frustration, I gave up on getting a response from the Novato Trane dealer, and began looking for another company.  Luckily, I discovered John Owens on Google, and after reading a number of reviews, gave them a call.

I explained our situation, and asked if someone could please come out to at least evaluate the problem.  They agreed to send a technician out that Friday, and Jared showed up right on schedule.  Once I turned the system on so that he could see and hear the problem, Jared took about 20 minutes to determine the cause, and make the necessary adjustments.  Turns out that the system's fan had been set for a 3-ton AC system, rather than our 2-ton system.  The fix seems to have been a simple one, at least for a technician who knows what he's doing. Jared was not only knowledgeable and efficient, but also very courteous and upbeat.  So, happily, we now have a Heating/AC system that works beautifully AND a new HVAC company - John Owens Services!</Text>

< Review>
So, to be fair, this is one of those instances where you don't do better until you know better (or in this case-tasted better). I thought the price was outstanding for the sandwich I received. However, I found that every time I would order the bread was so hard it would scrape the top of my mouth. Very uncomfortable, but I thought, " Hey, maybe this is how banh mi sandwiches are supposed to be". Then each time I went I would ask for extra jalape√±o. They would say okay sure, but I noticed a hesitation. When I got home there would be no extra and what's worse, I don't think they were using fresh ingredients because the "jalape√±os" were sweet not spicy. I even had to confirm that they were jalape√±os. Anyway, the sandwiches got soggier on the inside and harder on the outside. I finally tried Mai Banh Mi in Oakland. OH MY GOD. There's a sandwich! I only eat the vegetarian but the tofu was so much more flavorful, the bread was crisp and soft at the same time. The jalape√±os were fresh, even the cabbage tasted better. That's that on that. Peace out Loving Tea, stay blessed.</Review>

< Review>
I can see why there are so many varied reviews. This was my first time going to Church's Chicken since I was a kid. I can't complain too much! I was only in line for a hot minute, I ordered the three piece and a biscuit for 2.99 and they gave me an extra piece of chicken without my asking. The skin was really tasty and crispy, the meat itself could have cooked just a little bit longer for me and dried out just a little bit. The biscuit had great flavor-  I enjoy my food cooked a certain way, and the biscuit had an interesting little crisp to it which I really enjoyed, although I could totally understand if others might consider the biscuit too "hard"...The server was nice and a little silly, but he's just a kid so it was fine. Overall it was a nice first experience, would  I go back? Yes I would.<//Review>
